### In App Feedback

[Open in zeroheight](https://www.lightningdesignsystem.com/2e1ef8501/v/61481/p/67b473-in-app-feedback) — 23 image(s)

- `zeroheight-user-uploads.s3.eu-west-1.amazonaws.com` (markdown) *Link to the SLDS Figma library*
- `zeroheight-user-uploads.s3.eu-west-1.amazonaws.com` (markdown) *In this user journey: 
1: The user proactively chooses to give feedback OR is prompted by Salesforce.
2: The feedback mechanism appears.
3: Decision: Does the user engage with the mechanism? If yes, proceed to step 4. If no, proceed to step 7.
4: The user provides feedback.
5: Decision: Does the user want to join our research organization? If yes, proceed to step 6. If no, proceed to step 8.
6: An opt-in email for the research organization is sent.
7: The user ignores or dismisses the mechanism. It may reappear up to 3 times.
8: A "Thank you" message appears, and the in-app feedback process is complete.*
